***vermoorden.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vermoorden.html>vermoorden</a> (485)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">vermorden</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ver-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:moorden.html>moorden</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vermoorden.html>vermoorden</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to murder</li></ol>

<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">vermoording</span></li></ul>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">vernēmen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">farneman</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*franemaną</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ver-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:nemen.html>nemen</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vernietigingskamp.html>vernietigingskamp</a> (86686)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vernietiging.html>vernietiging</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kamp.html>kamp</a></i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vernietigingskamp.html>vernietigingskamp</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vernietigingskampen.html>vernietigingskampen</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>extermination camp, death camp <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">camp intended for the extermination of certain groups</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>The word <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> strong associations with the Second World War and with the Holocaust in particular.</li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:vernietigingskamp.html>vernietigingskamp</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic"><a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>o</a></span>
</p>

<p>Blend of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vermoeden.html>vermoeden</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:onderstellen.html>onderstellen</a></i> from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">onder-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stellen.html>stellen</a></i>, calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">suppōnō</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">unterstellen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to assume, to allege</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ver-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ongeluk.html>ongeluk</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.
</p>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> in an accident

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">reflexive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to afford, allow oneself
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heeft.html>heeft</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zo.html>zo</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:druk.html>druk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:zich.html>zich</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kan.html>kan</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:veroorloven.html>veroorloven</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:vakantie.html>vakantie</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nemen.html>nemen</a>.</i>
<dl><dd>He's so busy that he can'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> <b>afford</b> to take any holiday.</dd></dl></dd>
<dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:vrije.html>Vrije</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dag.html>dag</a>? <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>Dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kan.html>kan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tegenwoordig.html>tegenwoordig</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:veroorloven.html>veroorloven</a></b>!</i>
